## Page 408

### p408_default_t1 (default, high confidence)

|Manage System Access and Security|Col2|
|---|---|
||**Manage LDAP Servers**|



### p408_default_t2 (default, high confidence)

|Field|Description|
|---|---|
|Name|Name of the LDAP handler.|
|IP address/ Host name|LDAP server IP address or host name|
|Secure connection|Enable the** Secure Connection** toggle button if you want to connect to the LDAP<br>server via the SSL communication. When enabled, select the secure LDAP certificate<br>from the** Certificate** drop-down list.<br>**Note**<br>The secure LDAP certificate must be added in the Certificate Management screen<br>prior to configuring the secure LDAP server.<br>This field is disabled by default.|
|Port|The default LDAP port number is 389. If Secure Connection SSL is enabled, the default<br>LDAP port number is 636.|
|Bind DN|Enter the login access details to the database. Bind DN allows user to login to the<br>LDAP server.|
|Bind credential / Confirm<br>bind credential|Username and password to login to the LDAP server.|
|Base DN|Base DN is the starting point used by the LDAP server to search for user authentication<br>within your directory.|
|User filter|The filter for user search.|
|DN format|The format used to identify the user in base DN.|
|Principal attribute ID|This value represents the UID attribute in the LDAP server user profile under which<br>a particular username is organized.|
|Policy base DN|This value represents the role mapping for user roles within your directory.|
|Policy map attribute|This helps in identifying the user under the policy base DN.<br>This value maps to the` userFilter` parameter in your LDAP server attributes.|
|Policy ID|Enter the user role that you created in the LDAP server. The** Policy ID** is a unique key<br>used by the LDAP server to identify and retrieve the user role assigned to an<br>authenticated user. This value must exactly match the user role you configured on the<br>LDAP server.<br>In Crosswork Network Controller, this field corresponds to the_ policy_id_.<br>**Note**<br>If you try to login to Crosswork Network Controller as a LDAP user before creating<br>the required user role, you will get the error message:` "Login failed, policy`<br>`not found. Please contact the Network Administrator for`<br>`assistance."`. To avoid this error, ensure to create the relevant user roles in the<br>LDAP server, before setting up a new LDAP server in Crosswork.|



### p408_default_t3 (default, high confidence)

|Col1|Col2|Cisco Crosswork Network Controller 7.1 Administration Guide|

### p422_default_t1 (default, high confidence)

|Manage System Access and Security|Col2|
|---|---|
||**Configure a Trap Server**|



### p422_default_t2 (default, high confidence)

|Field|Description|Example|
|---|---|---|
|`Pri`|The priority of the event generated:<br>`Priority = (8*facility +`<br>`severity)`<br>Where` facility` is the category of<br>the event generated.<br>The category of the event generated<br>represented using an integer value:<br>`System = 3, Network = 7, Audit`<br>`= 13, Security = 4, External`<br>`= 1`<br>The alarm severity indicates the<br>severity of the event using an<br>integer value:<br>`Critical=2, Major=3,`<br>`Warning=4, Minor=5,`<br>`Info=6,Clear=7`|Event with the Category as System<br>and Severity as Major, the Pri = 8<br>* 3 + 3 = 27.|
|`v`|The version of the Syslog server.|NA|
|`Stamp`|The timestamp at which the event<br>is created.|`Mar 28 15:2:22 10.56.58.188`|
|`VIP`|The Crosswork VIP address.|`10.56.58.188`|
|`App`|The event OriginServiceId and<br>OriginAppId.|`orchestrator-capp-infra`|
|`PID`|The process ID.|NA|
|`Message ID`|The event ID.|`8586f9cf-d05d-4d94-ab62-27d7e808b5f6`|
|`Structured Data`|The event ObjectId and event type.|`robot-topo-svc-0`|
|`Message`|The description of the event.|`Restart of robot-topo-svc`<br>`successful.`|

|3|On the** Alarms** window only:<br>Click the** Actions** dropdown menu to perform one or more of these actions on the currently<br>selected alarms:<br>•** Acknowledge**: Marks the currently selected alarms as acknowledged.<br>•** Unacknowledge**: If any of the currently selected alarms have been acknowledged, restores<br>them to the unacknowledged state.<br>•** Clear**: Removes all currently selected alarms from the** Alarms** window.<br>•** Clear all of this condition**: Removes all currently selected alarms that share the same<br>condition.<br>•** Notes**: Lets you add a text note to all of the currently selected alarms.<br>Crosswork enables the** Actions** menu only until you select one or more alarms using the selection<br>box next to the** Alarm ID** column.|

|7|Click on** More Options** to specify whether you want to view all alerts or only the latest, and<br>how often to sync the alerts display with the Crosswork database.<br>If you uncheck the** Alarm History** or** Event History** checkbox, the list shows all alerts.<br>If you uncheck the** Auto Sync** checkbox, Crosswork pauses synchronization.<br>**Note**<br>In a geo HA deployment configured with dual stack, a loss of peer connectivity may cause<br>discrepancies in the Events display flow on the standby cluster. To address the peer connectivity<br>issue, perform the following steps:<br>**1.**<br>Complete the application installation on the active cluster before proceeding with the<br>installation on the standby cluster.<br>**2.**<br>In the** Events** window on the standby cluster, click on** More options** and uncheck the** View**<br>**latest events** option.|
|8|Click in the** Saved Views** field to manage the previously saved views created using the** Save**<br>**View** button. The popup** Manage Saved Views** window allows you to view, sort, see all views<br>or only those you have saved.|
|9|Click the** Save View** button to save the current view. Crosswork will prompt you to enter and<br>save the view under a unique name.|

|Recommendation|Do the following:<br>• Look at the job history and identify where in the<br>activation process it failed. If it fails at the start<br>of one of the pods coming up, restart the pods.<br>• Uninstall the application and then try installing<br>the application again.|



### p444_default_t4 (default, high confidence)

|---|---|

|cenCustomerRevision|SnmpAdminString|1.3.6.1.4.9.9.311.1.1.2.1.28|User input message.<br>The attribute takes in a<br>free format text.
